let S={ cluster:'ALL', channel:'ALL', metric:'GMV', tab:'cluster', // Overall MTD drill drill:{open:false, l1:null, l2:null}, // Per-store drill: {sid: {open:bool, l2:null|string}} storeDrill:{} }; /* ══ HELPERS ══ */ function getV(sd,ch,l1,period,metric){ if(!sd)return 0; const chs=ch==='ALL'?['POS','ECOM']:[ch]; const k=metric==='NOB'?'N':metric==='QTY'?'Q':'G'; return chs.reduce((s,c)=>{ const l1d=sd[c]&&sd[c][l1]; if(!l1d)return s; let t=0; for(const l2 in l1d){const pv=l1d[l2][period];if(pv)t+=pv[k]||0;} return s+t; },0); } function getL2V(sd,ch,l1,l2,period,metric){ if(!sd)return 0; const chs=ch==='ALL'?['POS','ECOM']:[ch]; const k=metric==='NOB'?'N':metric==='QTY'?'Q':'G'; return chs.reduce((s,c)=>{ const pv=sd[c]&&sd[c][l1]&&sd[c][l1][l2]&&sd[c][l1][l2][period]; return s+(pv?pv[k]||0:0); },0); } function fmt(v,m){ if(!v||isNaN(v)||v===0)return'—'; if(m==='GMV'){ if(v>=1e7)return'₹'+(v/1e7).toFixed(2)+'Cr'; if(v>=1e5)return'₹'+(v/1e5).toFixed(2)+'L'; if(v>=1e3)return'₹'+(v/1e3).toFixed(1)+'K'; return'₹'+Math.round(v); } // NOB and QTY: no rupee symbol if(v>=1e7)return(v/1e7).toFixed(2)+'Cr'; if(v>=1e5)return(v/1e5).toFixed(2)+'L'; if(v>=1e3)return(v/1e3).toFixed(1)+'K'; return(+v.toFixed(1)).toString(); } function fmtG(v){return fmt(v,'GMV');} function pctChg(c,p){if(!p||p===0)return null;return(c-p)/p*100;} function momBadge(c,p){ const d=pctChg(c,p); if(d===null)return'—'; const up=d>=0; return`${up?'▲':'▼'} ${Math.abs(d).toFixed(1)}%`; } function growBadge(c,p){ const d=pctChg(c,p); if(d===null)return{cls:'neu',lbl:'—',val:0,delta:0}; const delta=c-p; return d>=0?{cls:'grow',lbl:`▲ ${d.toFixed(1)}%`,val:d,delta}:{cls:'degrow',lbl:`▼ ${Math.abs(d).toFixed(1)}%`,val:d,delta}; } function allSites(){return Object.keys(D1).sort();} function getSiteCluster(sid){return D1[sid]?.cluster||SM[sid]?.c||'Others';} function getSiteName(sid){return D1[sid]?.name||SM[sid]?.n||sid;} function getSiteFn(sid){return D1[sid]?.fn||SM[sid]?.fn||'';} function getClusters(){ const s=new Set(); allSites().forEach(sid=>s.add(getSiteCluster(sid))); return['ALL',...Array.from(s).sort()]; } function getSites(cl){ return cl==='ALL'?allSites():allSites().filter(s=>getSiteCluster(s)===cl); } function sumObj(o){return Object.values(o).reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);} /* Cluster-level L1 aggregate */ function clusterL1(period){ const a={}; L1_CATS.forEach(l=>a[l]=0); for(const sid of getSites(S.cluster)) for(const l of L1_CATS) a[l]+=getV(D1[sid],S.channel,l,period,S.metric); return a; } /* Cluster-level L2 for May MTD vs Jun MTD */ function clusterL2(l1){ const res={}; const k=S.metric==='NOB'?'N':S.metric==='QTY'?'Q':'G'; for(const sid of getSites(S.cluster)){ const sd=D1[sid]; if(!sd)continue; const chs=S.channel==='ALL'?['POS','ECOM']:[S.channel]; for(const ch of chs){ const l1d=sd[ch]&&sd[ch][l1]; if(!l1d)continue; for(const l2 in l1d){ if(!res[l2])res[l2]={m:0,j:0}; const mv=l1d[l2]['may_mtd'],jv=l1d[l2]['jun_mtd']; res[l2].m+=(mv?mv[k]||0:0); res[l2].j+=(jv?jv[k]||0:0); } } } return res; } /* Store-level L2 for May MTD vs Jun MTD */ function storeL2(sid,l1){ const res={}; const k=S.metric==='NOB'?'N':S.metric==='QTY'?'Q':'G'; const sd=D1[sid]; if(!sd)return res; const chs=S.channel==='ALL'?['POS','ECOM']:[S.channel]; for(const ch of chs){ const l1d=sd[ch]&&sd[ch][l1]; if(!l1d)continue; for(const l2 in l1d){ if(!res[l2])res[l2]={m:0,j:0}; const mv=l1d[l2]['may_mtd'],jv=l1d[l2]['jun_mtd']; res[l2].m+=(mv?mv[k]||0:0); res[l2].j+=(jv?jv[k]||0:0); } } return res; } /* ══ BUILD UI ══ */ function buildUI(){ document.getElementById('liveLbl').textContent= new /* ══ KSIN TABLES (reusable) ══ */ function ksinDrillTables(ksinSource, l1, l2, metric, storeName){ // ksinSource: {ksin: {t, m:{N,G}, j:{N,G}}} const k=metric==='NOB'?'N':'G'; const rows=Object.entries(ksinSource) .map(([ksin,d])=>({ksin,title:d.t,m:d.m[k]||0,j:d.j[k]||0})) .filter(r=>r.m>0||r.j>0) .filter(r=>(r.title||'').trim().toUpperCase()!=='TOTAL') .filter(r=>l1!=='Consumables'); const grow=rows.filter(r=>r.j>=r.m).sort((a,b)=>(b.j-b.m)-(a.j-a.m)); // large Δ first const degrow=rows.filter(r=>r.j(a.j-a.m)-(b.j-b.m)); // largest degrow first const makeTable=(arr,label,isGrow)=>{ if(!arr.length)return''; const col=isGrow?'#059669':'#b91c1c'; const bg=isGrow?'linear-gradient(135deg,#064e3b,#059669)':'linear-gradient(135deg,#450a0a,#b91c1c)'; return`
${isGrow?'📈 Grow SKUs — largest gain first':'📉 Degrow SKUs — largest loss first'}
${storeName?`${storeName} · `:''}${l1} › ${l2}  ·  ${arr.length} SKUs  ·  sorted by |Δ| ${isGrow?'largest gain':'largest loss'} first
${arr.map(r=>{ const b=growBadge(r.j,r.m); const delta=r.j-r.m; return``; }).join('')}
Product (KSIN) May MTDJun MTD Change %Shrinkage
${r.title||r.ksin}
KSIN: ${r.ksin}
 ${fmt(r.m,metric)} ${fmt(r.j,metric)} ${b.lbl} ${delta>=0?'+':''}${fmt(Math.abs(delta),metric)}
SUBTOTAL (${arr.length}) ${fmt(arr.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.m,0),metric)} ${fmt(arr.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.j,0),metric)} ${momBadge(arr.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.j,0),arr.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.m,0))}
`; }; return makeTable(degrow,'',false) + makeTable(grow,'',true); } /* ══ L2 DRILL TABLE (degrow→grow sorted) ══ */ function l2DrillBlock(l2map, l1, onClickFn, activeL2, closeId, storeName, metric){ metric=metric||S.metric; const entries=Object.entries(l2map).filter(([,v])=>v.m>0||v.j>0); // Sort: degrow first (largest loss → smallest), then grow (largest gain first) entries.sort((a,b)=>{ const da=a[1].j-a[1].m, db=b[1].j-b[1].m; // both degrow: larger loss first (more negative = smaller da) if(da<0&&db<0)return da-db; // both grow: larger gain first if(da>=0&&db>=0)return db-da; // degrow before grow return da<0?-1:1; }); const grow=entries.filter(([,v])=>v.j>=v.m); const degrow=entries.filter(([,v])=>v.js+v.m,0),j:entries.reduce((s,[,v])=>s+v.j,0)}; const makeSection=(arr,isGrow)=>{ if(!arr.length)return''; const secBg=isGrow?'#f0fdf4':'#fff5f5'; const col=isGrow?'#16a34a':'#dc2626'; return`${isGrow?'▲ GROW':'▼ DEGROW'} (${arr.length}) ${arr.map(([l2,v])=>{ const b=growBadge(v.j,v.m); const sel=activeL2===l2; return` ${isGrow?'📈':'📉'}${l2}🔍 ${fmt(v.m,metric)} ${fmt(v.j,metric)} ${b.lbl} ${v.j>=v.m?'+':''}${fmt(Math.abs(v.j-v.m),metric)} `; }).join('')}`; }; return`
📊 L2 Breakdown — ${l1} · May MTD vs Jun MTD${storeName?`  ·  🏪 ${storeName}`:''}
Sorted: Degrow (largest loss first) → Grow (largest gain first)  ·  ✕ Close
${makeSection(degrow,false)} ${makeSection(grow,true)}
L2 Category May MTDJun MTD Change %Shrinkage
TOTAL ${fmt(l2Tot.m,metric)}${fmt(l2Tot.j,metric)} ${momBadge(l2Tot.j,l2Tot.m)}
`; } /* ══ RENDER ══ */ function render(){ const marA=clusterL1('mar_full'), aprA=clusterL1('apr_full'), mayFA=clusterL1('may_full'), mayMA=clusterL1('may_mtd'), junA=clusterL1('jun_mtd'); const [marT,aprT,mFT,mMT,jT]=[marA,aprA,mayFA,mayMA,junA].map(sumObj); let h=''; /* ── OPEN INSIGHTS TAB (renders first, no cards) ── */ if(S.tab==='insights'){ var suggs=[ {icon:'🍎',label:'Top KSINs in Fruits',q:'top 10 ksin in Fruits'}, {icon:'📉',label:'Most declining stores',q:'bottom 10 stores declining'}, {icon:'🏆',label:'Best store Jun MTD',q:'top 5 stores best performing'}, {icon:'🌿',label:'Top Vegetables KSINs',q:'top 10 ksin in Vegetables'}, {icon:'🔄',label:'Cluster comparison',q:'compare all clusters'}, {icon:'🛒',label:'Staples top products',q:'top 10 ksin in Staples'}, {icon:'📦',label:'FMCG Food growth',q:'growing categories in FMCG Food'}, {icon:'🏪',label:'Ananth cluster top stores',q:'top 5 stores in Ananth cluster'}, ]; var pillsHtml=''; for(var si=0;si' +suggs[si].icon+' '+suggs[si].label+''; } h+='' +'

},50); } function drillL2(l2){ S.drill.l2=S.drill.l2===l2?null:l2; render(); if(S.drill.l2)setTimeout(()=>{ document.querySelector('[style*="border:2px solid #b91c1c"],[style*="border:2px solid #059669"]') ?.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'}); },50); } function closeDrill(){S.drill={open:false,l1:null,l2:null};render();} /* ══ DRILL CONTROLS — STORE LEVEL ══ */ function storeDrillL1(sid,l1){ if(!S.storeDrill[sid])S.storeDrill[sid]={open:false,l1:null,l2:null}; const ds=S.storeDrill[sid]; if(ds.open&&ds.l1===l1){S.storeDrill[sid]={open:false,l1:null,l2:null};} else{S.storeDrill[sid]={open:true,l1:l1,l2:null};} render(); setTimeout(()=>{ document.querySelector(`[id="closeStore_${sid}"]`)?.parentElement ?.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'}); },80); } function storeDrillL2(sid,l1,l2){ if(!S.storeDrill[sid])S.storeDrill[sid]={open:true,l1:l1,l2:null}; const ds=S.storeDrill[sid]; ds.l2=ds.l2===l2?null:l2; ds.l1=l1; ds.open=true; render(); setTimeout(()=>{ const els=document.querySelectorAll('[style*="border:2px solid #b91c1c"],[style*="border:2px solid #059669"]'); if(els.length)els[els.length-1].scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'}); },80); } function storeDrillClose(sid){S.storeDrill[sid]={open:false,l1:null,l2:null};render();} /* ══ FILTER CONTROLS ══ */ function setTab(t){ S.tab=t; // Toggle order: [0]=Gowtham_TT, [1]=Cluster View document.querySelectorAll('.ctrlbar .pg:first-child .pill').forEach((b,i)=>b.classList.toggle('on', (t==='cluster'&&i===0)||(t==='report'&&i===1))); if(t==='report'){ // Auto-select first cluster when switching to Cluster View const clusters=getClusters().filter(c=>c!=='ALL'); if(clusters.length){ const target=S.cluster==='ALL'?clusters[0]:S.cluster; S.cluster=target; document.querySelectorAll('#clPills .pill').forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('on',b.textContent===target)); } S.drill={open:false,l1:null,l2:null}; S.storeDrill={}; render(); } else if(t==='insights'){ S.drill={open:false,l1:null,l2:null}; S.storeDrill={}; document.querySelectorAll('.ctrlbar .pg:first-child .pill').forEach((b,i)=> b.classList.toggle('on',i===2)); render(); } else { // Gowtham_TT: clear cluster selection, reset drills S.cluster='ALL'; S.drill={open:false,l1:null,l2:null}; S.storeDrill={}; document.querySelectorAll('#clPills .pill').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('on')); render(); } } function setCluster(c){ S.cluster=c; S.drill={open:false,l1:null,l2:null}; S.storeDrill={}; // Auto-switch to Cluster View when a cluster is clicked if(c!=='ALL'&&S.tab==='cluster'){ S.tab='report'; document.querySelectorAll('.ctrlbar .pg:first-child .pill').forEach((b,i)=> b.classList.toggle('on',i===1)); } document.querySelectorAll('#clPills .pill').forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('on',b.textContent===c)); render(); } function setCh(c){ S.channel=c; ['OMNI','POS','ECOM'].forEach(id=>{ const btn=document.getElementById('chPill'+id); if(btn) btn.classList.toggle('on',(c==='ALL'&&id==='OMNI')||(c!=='ALL'&&id===c)); }); render(); } function setM(m){ S.metric=m; document.querySelectorAll('#metricPills .pill').forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('on',b.textContent===m)); render(); } /* ══ AI INSIGHTS ══ */ function buildInsightContext(){ // Build a compact data summary for the AI const clusters=getClusters().filter(c=>c!=='ALL'); const lines=[]; lines.push('KPN Fresh Dashboard Data Summary (May MTD vs Jun MTD):'); lines.push('Metric: '+S.metric+' | Channel: '+(S.channel==='ALL'?'OMNI':S.channel)); clusters.forEach(cl=>{ const sites=[...getSites(cl)]; const mm=L1_CATS.reduce((s,l)=>s+sites.reduce((ss,sid)=>ss+getV(D1[sid],S.channel,l,'may_mtd',S.metric),0),0); const jj=L1_CATS.reduce((s,l)=>s+sites.reduce((ss,sid)=>ss+getV(D1[sid],S.channel,l,'jun_mtd',S.metric),0),0); const pct=mm?((jj-mm)/mm*100):0; lines.push(`Cluster ${cl}: ${sites.length} stores, May=${fmt(mm,S.metric)} Jun=${fmt(jj,S.metric)} Δ=${pct.toFixed(1)}%`); L1_CATS.forEach(l=>{ const lm=sites.reduce((s,sid)=>s+getV(D1[sid],S.channel,l,'may_mtd',S.metric),0); const lj=sites.reduce((s,sid)=>s+getV(D1[sid],S.channel,l,'jun_mtd',S.metric),0); if(lm||lj) lines.push(` ${l}: May=${fmt(lm,S.metric)} Jun=${fmt(lj,S.metric)}`); }); }); // Add top/bottom stores const allSites2=[...getSites('ALL')]; const ranked=allSites2.map(sid=>{ const jj=L1_CATS.reduce((s,l)=>s+getV(D1[sid],S.channel,l,'jun_mtd',S.metric),0); const mm=L1_CATS.reduce((s,l)=>s+getV(D1[sid],S.channel,l,'may_mtd',S.metric),0); return{sid,name:getSiteName(sid),jj,mm,pct:mm?((jj-mm)/mm*100):0}; }).sort((a,b)=>b.pct-a.pct); lines.push('Top 3 stores (MoM %): '+ranked.slice(0,3).map(r=>`${r.name}(${r.pct.toFixed(1)}%)`).join(', ')); lines.push('Bottom 3 stores (MoM %): '+ranked.slice(-3).map(r=>`${r.name}(${r.pct.toFixed(1)}%)`).join(', ')); return lines.join('\n'); } /* ══ DUCKDB-WASM ENGINE ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ Runs entirely in the browser — no server, no API key. Parquet files (store_metrics.parquet, ksin_metrics.parquet) must be in the same folder as index.html (or same GitHub Pages repo root). ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */ var _db = null; var _dbReady = false; var _dbLoading = false; var _dbCallbacks = []; async function initDuckDB() { if (_dbReady) return _db; if (_dbLoading) { return new Promise(function(res){ _dbCallbacks.push(res); }); } _dbLoading = true; // Load DuckDB-WASM from CDN const CDN = 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@duckdb/duckdb-wasm@1.29.0/dist/'; const BUNDLES = { mvp: { mainModule: CDN+'duckdb-mvp.wasm', mainWorker: CDN+'duckdb-browser-mvp.worker.js' }, eh: { mainModule: CDN+'duckdb-eh.wasm', mainWorker: CDN+'duckdb-browser-eh.worker.js' }, }; await new Promise(function(res,rej){ var s = document.createElement('script'); s.src = CDN + 'duckdb-browser.cjs.js'; s.onload = res; s.onerror = rej; document.head.appendChild(s); }); const duckdb = window.duckdb; const bundle = await duckdb.selectBundle(BUNDLES); const workerUrl = URL.createObjectURL( new Blob(['importScripts("'+bundle.mainWorker+'")'], {type:'text/javascript'}) ); const worker = new Worker(workerUrl); const logger = new duckdb.ConsoleLogger(); const db = new duckdb.AsyncDuckDB(logger, worker); await db.instantiate(bundle.mainModule, CDN+'duckdb-browser.cjs.js'); const conn = await db.connect(); // Determine base URL for parquet files (works on GitHub Pages and localhost) const base = (location.href.replace(/\/[^/]*$/, '') + '/'); // Load parquet files await conn.query("INSTALL httpfs; LOAD httpfs;"); await conn.query("CREATE TABLE store_metrics AS SELECT * FROM read_parquet('"+base+"store_metrics.parquet')"); await conn.query("CREATE TABLE ksin_metrics AS SELECT * FROM read_parquet('"+base+"ksin_metrics.parquet')"); await conn.close(); _db = db; _dbReady = true; _dbLoading = false; _dbCallbacks.forEach(function(cb){ cb(db); }); _dbCallbacks = []; return db; } async function dbQuery(sql) { var db = await initDuckDB(); var conn = await db.connect(); var result = await conn.query(sql); await conn.close(); // Convert Arrow table to plain array of objects var schema = result.schema.fields.map(function(f){ return f.name; }); var rows = []; for (var i = 0; i < result.numRows; i++) { var row = {}; schema.forEach(function(col){ var val = result.getChildAt(schema.indexOf(col)).get(i); row[col] = (val !== null && val !== undefined) ? Number(val) || String(val) : null; }); rows.push(row); } return rows; } /* ── FORMAT HELPERS ── */ function fmtV(v, metric) { if (!v || isNaN(v) || v === 0) return '—'; if (metric === 'gmv') { if (v >= 1e7) return '₹'+(v/1e7).toFixed(2)+'Cr'; if (v >= 1e5) return '₹'+(v/1e5).toFixed(2)+'L'; if (v >= 1e3) return '₹'+(v/1e3).toFixed(1)+'K'; return '₹'+Math.round(v); } if (v >= 1e5) return (v/1e5).toFixed(2)+'L'; if (v >= 1e3) return (v/1e3).toFixed(1)+'K'; return Math.round(v).toString(); } function pctStr(a, b) { if (!b) return '0.0%'; var p = ((a - b) / b * 100).toFixed(1); return (p >= 0 ? '+' : '') + p + '%'; } function trend(a, b) { return a >= b ? '📈' : '📉'; } function badgeClr(pct) { return pct && pct.startsWith('-') ? '#f87171' : '#4ade80'; } function badgeBg(pct) { return pct && pct.startsWith('-') ? '#450a0a' : '#052e16'; } /* ══ AI INSIGHTS (DuckDB-powered, no API) ══ */ /* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ OPEN-SOURCE AI INSIGHTS ENGINE Runs 100% in the browser — no API key, no server. Uses D1/D2 data already embedded in the page + DuckDB-WASM for Open Insights. ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */ /* ── FORMAT HELPERS ── */ function fmtV(v, metric) { if (!v || isNaN(v) || v === 0) return '—'; if (metric === 'gmv') { if (v >= 1e7) return '₹'+(v/1e7).toFixed(2)+'Cr'; if (v >= 1e5) return '₹'+(v/1e5).toFixed(2)+'L'; if (v >= 1e3) return '₹'+(v/1e3).toFixed(1)+'K'; return '₹'+Math.round(v); } if (v >= 1e5) return (v/1e5).toFixed(2)+'L'; if (v >= 1e3) return (v/1e3).toFixed(1)+'K'; return Math.round(v).toString(); } function pctChgStr(a, b) { if (!b) return '0.0%'; var p = ((a - b) / b * 100).toFixed(1); return (p >= 0 ? '+' : '') + p + '%'; } function trendIcon(a, b) { return a >= b ? '📈' : '📉'; } function badgeClr(a, b) { return a >= b ? '#4ade80' : '#f87171'; } function badgeBg(a, b) { return a >= b ? '#052e16' : '#450a0a'; } /* ── D1 AGGREGATION HELPERS (use embedded data, no DuckDB needed) ── */ function allSiteIds() { return Object.keys(D1).filter(function(s){ return D1[s] && D1[s].name; }); } function siteVal(sid, channel, l1, period, metric) { var sd = D1[sid]; if (!sd) return 0; var channels = channel === 'ALL' ? ['POS','ECOM'] : [channel]; var total = 0; channels.forEach(function(ch) { if (!sd[ch]) return; if (l1 === 'ALL') { Object.keys(sd[ch]).forEach(function(cat) { Object.keys(sd[ch][cat] || {}).forEach(function(l2) { var p = (sd[ch][cat][l2] || {})[period]; if (p) total += (metric==='nob'?p.N:metric==='qty'?p.Q:p.G)||0; }); }); } else { Object.keys(sd[ch][l1] || {}).forEach(function(l2) { var p = (sd[ch][l1][l2] || {})[period]; if (p) total += (metric==='nob'?p.N:metric==='qty'?p.Q:p.G)||0; }); } }); return total; } function clusterVal(cluster, period, metric) { var sites = cluster === 'ALL' ? allSiteIds() : allSiteIds().filter(function(s){ return D1[s].cluster === cluster; }); return sites.reduce(function(sum, sid){ return sum + siteVal(sid, 'ALL', 'ALL', period, metric); }, 0); } function l1Val(l1cat, cluster, period, metric) { var sites = cluster === 'ALL' ? allSiteIds() : allSiteIds().filter(function(s){ return D1[s].cluster === cluster; }); return sites.reduce(function(sum, sid){ return sum + siteVal(sid, 'ALL', l1cat, period, metric); }, 0); } /* ══ AI INSIGHTS (fully open-source, uses D1 data) ══ */ function loadAIInsights(containerId) { var el = document.getElementById(containerId); if (!el) return; if (el.dataset.loaded === '1') return; el.dataset.loaded = '1'; el.innerHTML = '
⚙️ Computing insights...
'; setTimeout(function() { try { var metric = S.metric.toLowerCase(); var cluster = (S.cluster && S.cluster !== 'ALL') ? S.cluster : 'ALL'; var scope = cluster === 'ALL' ? 'All Stores' : cluster + ' Cluster'; var insights = []; // ── 1. Overall MoM trend var mv = clusterVal(cluster, 'may_mtd', metric); var jv = clusterVal(cluster, 'jun_mtd', metric); var p1 = pctChgStr(jv, mv); var mood = parseFloat(p1) > 5 ? 'Strong growth momentum.' : parseFloat(p1) > 0 ? 'Marginal growth.' : 'Declining — needs attention.'; insights.push(trendIcon(jv,mv)+' Overall '+metric.toUpperCase()+' for '+scope+': May MTD '+fmtV(mv,metric)+' → Jun MTD '+fmtV(jv,metric)+' ('+p1+' MoM). '+mood); // ── 2. Best L1 category var bestL1 = null, bestPct = -Infinity; L1_CATS.forEach(function(cat) { var lmv = l1Val(cat, cluster, 'may_mtd', metric); var ljv = l1Val(cat, cluster, 'jun_mtd', metric); if (lmv > 0) { var p = (ljv-lmv)/lmv*100; if (p > bestPct) { bestPct=p; bestL1={cat:cat,mv:lmv,jv:ljv,p:p}; } } }); if (bestL1) { insights.push('🌟 Best category: '+bestL1.cat+' grew from '+fmtV(bestL1.mv,metric)+' → '+fmtV(bestL1.jv,metric)+' (+'+bestL1.p.toFixed(1)+'% MoM).'+(bestL1.p>10?' Strong momentum — maintain stocking & promos.':' Consistent performer.')); } // ── 3. Worst L1 category var worstL1 = null, worstPct = Infinity; L1_CATS.forEach(function(cat) { var lmv = l1Val(cat, cluster, 'may_mtd', metric); var ljv = l1Val(cat, cluster, 'jun_mtd', metric); if (lmv > 0) { var p = (ljv-lmv)/lmv*100; if (p < worstPct) { worstPct=p; worstL1={cat:cat,mv:lmv,jv:ljv,p:p}; } } }); if (worstL1 && worstL1.p < 0) { insights.push('⚠️ Risk category: '+worstL1.cat+' declined '+worstL1.p.toFixed(1)+'% (May '+fmtV(worstL1.mv,metric)+' → Jun '+fmtV(worstL1.jv,metric)+'). Investigate demand, pricing or supply issues.'); } // ── 4. Top store by MoM % var topStore = null, topPct = -Infinity; allSiteIds().forEach(function(sid) { if (cluster !== 'ALL' && D1[sid].cluster !== cluster) return; var smv = siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','may_mtd',metric); var sjv = siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','jun_mtd',metric); if (smv > 0) { var sp = (sjv-smv)/smv*100; if (sp > topPct) { topPct=sp; topStore={name:D1[sid].name,cluster:D1[sid].cluster,mv:smv,jv:sjv,p:sp}; } } }); if (topStore) { insights.push('🏆 Top store: '+topStore.name+' ('+topStore.cluster+') — Jun MTD '+fmtV(topStore.jv,metric)+' ('+pctChgStr(topStore.jv,topStore.mv)+' MoM). Benchmark best practices from this store.'); } // ── 5. Most declining store var botStore = null, botPct = Infinity; allSiteIds().forEach(function(sid) { if (cluster !== 'ALL' && D1[sid].cluster !== cluster) return; var smv = siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','may_mtd',metric); var sjv = siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','jun_mtd',metric); if (smv > 0) { var sp = (sjv-smv)/smv*100; if (sp < botPct) { botPct=sp; botStore={name:D1[sid].name,cluster:D1[sid].cluster,mv:smv,jv:sjv,p:sp}; } } }); if (botStore && botStore.p < 0) { insights.push('🔴 Needs action: '+botStore.name+' ('+botStore.cluster+') declining '+botStore.p.toFixed(1)+'% (May '+fmtV(botStore.mv,metric)+' → Jun '+fmtV(botStore.jv,metric)+'). Escalate to cluster manager for immediate review.'); } // ── 6. Channel split (POS vs ECOM) var sites = cluster === 'ALL' ? allSiteIds() : allSiteIds().filter(function(s){ return D1[s].cluster===cluster; }); var posJ=0, ecomJ=0; sites.forEach(function(sid) { posJ += siteVal(sid,'POS','ALL','jun_mtd',metric); ecomJ += siteVal(sid,'ECOM','ALL','jun_mtd',metric); }); var total = posJ+ecomJ; if (total > 0) { insights.push('📊 Channel split (Jun MTD): POS '+fmtV(posJ,metric)+' ('+(posJ/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%) vs ECOM '+fmtV(ecomJ,metric)+' ('+(ecomJ/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%). '+(ecomJ/total>0.3?'ECOM growing well — invest in digital.':'POS dominant — ECOM has growth opportunity.')); } // ── 7. Cluster champion (only for ALL view) if (cluster === 'ALL') { var clusters = ['Ananth','Mahesh','Alagiri','Hinduraj P','Hari Govindan']; var champCluster = null, champPct = -Infinity; clusters.forEach(function(cl) { var cmv = clusterVal(cl,'may_mtd',metric); var cjv = clusterVal(cl,'jun_mtd',metric); if (cmv>0) { var cp=(cjv-cmv)/cmv*100; if(cp>champPct){champPct=cp; champCluster={name:cl,mv:cmv,jv:cjv,p:cp};} } }); if (champCluster) { insights.push('🥇 Best cluster: '+champCluster.name+' leads with '+champCluster.p.toFixed(1)+'% MoM growth (Jun MTD '+fmtV(champCluster.jv,metric)+'). Share playbook across other clusters.'); } } var html = insights.map(function(line) { return '
' + line.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1') + '
'; }).join(''); el.innerHTML = '
'+html+'
'; } catch(e) { el.innerHTML = '
⚠️ '+e.message+'
'; el.dataset.loaded = ''; } }, 10); } /* ══ OPEN INSIGHTS — NLP + DuckDB-WASM ══ */ var OI_CLUSTERS = ['Ananth','Mahesh','Alagiri','Hinduraj P','Hari Govindan']; var OI_L1 = ['Fruits','Vegetables','FMCG Food','FMCG Non Food','Staples','Poultry','KPN Cafe','Others']; function oiDetect(q, list) { return list.filter(function(x){ return q.toLowerCase().indexOf(x.toLowerCase()) >= 0; }); } function oiMetric(q) { var ql = q.toLowerCase(); if (/\bnob\b|order/.test(ql)) return 'nob'; if (/\bqty\b|quantity/.test(ql)) return 'qty'; return 'gmv'; } function oiLimit(q) { var m = q.match(/\b(\d+)\b/); if (m) { var n=parseInt(m[1]); if(n>=1&&n<=50) return n; } return 10; } function oiIntent(q) { var ql = q.toLowerCase(); if (/declin|degrow|drop|worst|bottom|lowest|poor|loss/.test(ql)) return 'degrow'; if (/ksin|sku|product|item/.test(ql)) return 'ksin'; if (/compar|vs |versus/.test(ql)) return 'compare'; if (/cluster|zone/.test(ql)) return 'cluster'; if (/store|branch|outlet/.test(ql)) return 'store'; return 'top'; } /* ── Pure JS fallback query engine (no DuckDB-WASM needed) ── */ function oiQueryJS(q) { var metric = oiMetric(q); var intent = oiIntent(q); var limit = oiLimit(q); var clusters = oiDetect(q, OI_CLUSTERS); var l1s = oiDetect(q, OI_L1); var order = intent === 'degrow' ? 1 : -1; var label = intent === 'degrow' ? 'Bottom' : 'Top'; var sites = allSiteIds().filter(function(sid) { return clusters.length === 0 || clusters.indexOf(D1[sid].cluster) >= 0; }); // ── KSIN query if (intent === 'ksin' || /ksin|sku|product|item/.test(q.toLowerCase()) || l1s.length) { var ksinRows = []; sites.forEach(function(sid) { if (!D2[sid]) return; var l1map = D2[sid]; Object.keys(l1map).forEach(function(l1) { if (l1s.length && l1s.indexOf(l1) < 0) return; Object.keys(l1map[l1]).forEach(function(l2) { Object.keys(l1map[l1][l2]).forEach(function(ksin) { var kd = l1map[l1][l2][ksin]; var mv = (kd.m||{})[metric==='nob'?'N':'G'] || 0; var jv = (kd.j||{})[metric==='nob'?'N':'G'] || 0; ksinRows.push({ name:kd.t||ksin, ksin:ksin, store:D1[sid].name, cluster:D1[sid].cluster, l1:l1, l2:l2, mv:mv, jv:jv, delta:jv-mv }); }); }); }); }); ksinRows.sort(function(a,b){ return order*(b.delta-a.delta); }); ksinRows = ksinRows.slice(0, limit); return { title: label+' '+limit+' KSINs'+(l1s.length?' in '+l1s.join(', '):'')+(clusters.length?' — '+clusters.join(', '):''), type: 'ksin', rows: ksinRows, metric: metric }; } // ── CLUSTER comparison if (intent === 'cluster' || intent === 'compare') { var clList = clusters.length ? clusters : OI_CLUSTERS; var clRows = clList.map(function(cl) { var clSites = allSiteIds().filter(function(s){ return D1[s].cluster===cl; }); var mv = clSites.reduce(function(s,sid){ return s+siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','may_mtd',metric); },0); var jv = clSites.reduce(function(s,sid){ return s+siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','jun_mtd',metric); },0); return { name:cl, stores:clSites.length, mv:mv, jv:jv }; }); clRows.sort(function(a,b){ return order*((b.jv-b.mv)/b.mv-(a.jv-a.mv)/a.mv); }); return { title:'Cluster Performance — May MTD vs Jun MTD · '+metric.toUpperCase(), type:'cluster', rows:clRows, metric:metric }; } // ── STORE ranking (default) var storeRows = sites.map(function(sid) { var mv = siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','may_mtd',metric); var jv = siteVal(sid,'ALL','ALL','jun_mtd',metric); return { name:D1[sid].name, cluster:D1[sid].cluster, mv:mv, jv:jv }; }).filter(function(r){ return r.mv>0; }); storeRows.sort(function(a,b){ return order*((b.jv-b.mv)/b.mv-(a.jv-a.mv)/a.mv); }); storeRows = storeRows.slice(0, limit); return { title: label+' '+limit+' Stores by MoM % · '+metric.toUpperCase()+(clusters.length?' — '+clusters.join(', '):''), type:'store', rows:storeRows, metric:metric }; } function oiRenderResult(data) { var resEl = document.getElementById('oiResult'); if (!resEl) return; var rows = data.rows || []; if (!rows.length) { resEl.innerHTML='
No results found.
'; return; } var metric = data.metric; var html = '
📊 '+data.title +''+rows.length+' results
'; html += '
'; if (data.type === 'ksin') { html += ''; rows.forEach(function(r,i) { var clr=badgeClr(r.jv,r.mv); var bg=badgeBg(r.jv,r.mv); var p=pctChgStr(r.jv,r.mv); html += '' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +''; }); } else if (data.type === 'cluster') { html += ''; rows.forEach(function(r,i) { var clr=badgeClr(r.jv,r.mv); var bg=badgeBg(r.jv,r.mv); var p=pctChgStr(r.jv,r.mv); html += '' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +''; }); } else { html += ''; rows.forEach(function(r,i) { var clr=badgeClr(r.jv,r.mv); var bg=badgeBg(r.jv,r.mv); var p=pctChgStr(r.jv,r.mv); html += '' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +'' +''; }); } html += '
#ProductKSINStoreL2May MTDJun MTDΔ%
'+(i+1)+''+(r.name||r.ksin)+''+r.ksin+''+r.store+''+r.l2+''+fmtV(r.mv,metric)+''+fmtV(r.jv,metric)+''+(r.delta>=0?'+':'')+fmtV(Math.abs(r.delta),metric)+''+trendIcon(r.jv,r.mv)+' '+p+'
#ClusterStoresMay MTDJun MTDGrowth
'+(i+1)+''+r.name+''+r.stores+''+fmtV(r.mv,metric)+''+fmtV(r.jv,metric)+''+trendIcon(r.jv,r.mv)+' '+p+'
